    44                              <1> ;--------------------Op Macros--------------------------
    45                              <1> 
    46                              <1> %macro vV_push 1
    47                              <1> 
    48                              <1> 	mov DWORD[vV_sp] , %1
    49                              <1> 	add vV_sp , 4
    50                              <1> 
    51                              <1> %endmacro
    52                              <1> 
    53                              <1> %macro vV_pop 1
    54                              <1> 
    55                              <1> 	sub vV_sp , 4
    56                              <1> 	mov %1 , [vV_sp]
    57                              <1> 	
    58                              <1> %endmacro
    59                              <1> 
    60                              <1> %macro vV_swap 0
    61                              <1> 
    62                              <1> 	mov edx , [vV_sp-4]
    63                              <1> 	mov eax , [vV_sp-8]
    64                              <1> 	mov [vV_sp-8] , edx 
    65                              <1> 	mov [vV_sp-4] , eax 
    66                              <1> 	
    67                              <1> %endmacro
    68                              <1> 
    69                              <1> %macro vV_dup 1
    70                              <1> 
    71                              <1> 	mov ecx , %1
    72                              <1> 	lea rsi , [vV_sp-cell(%1)]
    73                              <1> 	mov rdi , vV_sp
    74                              <1> 		
    75                              <1> 	rep movsd
    76                              <1> 	
    77                              <1> 	add vV_sp , cell(%1)
    78                              <1> 	
    79                              <1> %endmacro
    80                              <1> 
    81                              <1> 
    82                              <1> %macro vV_dec_sp 1
    83                              <1> 
    84                              <1> 	sub vV_sp , cell(%1)
    85                              <1> 	
    86                              <1> %endmacro
    87                              <1>
